<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>COSTCO WHOLESALE CORPORATION REPORTS FOURTH QUARTER AND FISCAL </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>YEAR 2019 OPERATING RESULTS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ISSAQUAH,
Wash., October&nbsp;3, 2019 - Costco Wholesale Corporation (&#147;Costco&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: COST) today announced its operating results for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">16-week</FONT> fourth quarter and the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">52-week</FONT> fiscal year, ended September&nbsp;1, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales for the quarter were $46.45&nbsp;billion, an increase of
7.0&nbsp;percent from $43.41&nbsp;billion during the similar period last year. Net sales for the fiscal year were $149.35&nbsp;billion, an increase of 7.9&nbsp;percent from $138.43&nbsp;billion during the similar period last year. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable sales for the fourth quarter and the fiscal year were as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">*</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Excluding the impacts from changes in gasoline prices, foreign exchange, and a previously disclosed accounting
change concerning revenue recognition (ASC 606). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income for the fourth quarter was $1,097&nbsp;million, or $2.47 per diluted share,
compared to $1,043&nbsp;million, or $2.36 per diluted share, last year. This year&#146;s fourth quarter was negatively impacted by a $123&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> reserve to SG&amp;A ($96&nbsp;million <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax),</FONT> or 22 cents per diluted share, related to a product tax assessment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income for the fiscal year was
$3.66&nbsp;billion, or $8.26 per diluted share, compared to $3.13&nbsp;billion, or $7.09 per diluted share, in the prior year. As previously disclosed and mentioned above, this year&#146;s net income was impacted by a net benefit of $30&nbsp;million
or $0.07 per diluted share from primarily <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items. Last year was positively impacted by a first quarter tax benefit of $41&nbsp;million or $0.09 per diluted share. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Costco currently operates 783 warehouses, including 544 in the United States and Puerto Rico, 100 in Canada, 39 in Mexico, 29 in the United Kingdom, 26 in
Japan, 16 in Korea, 13 in Taiwan, 11 in Australia, two in Spain, one in France, one in Iceland, and one in China. Costco also operates <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> web sites in the U.S., Canada, the United Kingdom, Mexico,
Korea and Taiwan. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A conference call to discuss these results is scheduled for 2:00 p.m. (PT) today, October&nbsp;3, 2019, and is available via a webcast
on www.costco.com (click on Investor Relations and &#147;Play Webcast&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain statements contained in this document constitute forward-looking
statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. For these purposes, forward-looking statements are statements that address activities, events, conditions or developments that the Company expects or anticipates
may occur in the future. In some cases forward-looking statements can be identified because they contain words </P>
